set -e;  echo '  LD      arch/x86/purgatory/purgatory.ro'; ld -m elf_x86_64  -z max-page-size=0x200000   -e purgatory_start -r --no-undefined -nostdlib -z nodefaultlib arch/x86/purgatory/purgatory.o arch/x86/purgatory/stack.o arch/x86/purgatory/setup-x86_64.o arch/x86/purgatory/sha256.o arch/x86/purgatory/entry64.o arch/x86/purgatory/string.o -o arch/x86/purgatory/purgatory.ro; printf '%s\n' 'cmd_arch/x86/purgatory/purgatory.ro := ld -m elf_x86_64  -z max-page-size=0x200000   -e purgatory_start -r --no-undefined -nostdlib -z nodefaultlib arch/x86/purgatory/purgatory.o arch/x86/purgatory/stack.o arch/x86/purgatory/setup-x86_64.o arch/x86/purgatory/sha256.o arch/x86/purgatory/entry64.o arch/x86/purgatory/string.o -o arch/x86/purgatory/purgatory.ro' > arch/x86/purgatory/.purgatory.ro.cmd
set -e;  echo '  BIN2C   arch/x86/purgatory/kexec-purgatory.c'; ./scripts/bin2c kexec_purgatory < arch/x86/purgatory/purgatory.ro > arch/x86/purgatory/kexec-purgatory.c; printf '%s\n' 'cmd_arch/x86/purgatory/kexec-purgatory.c := ./scripts/bin2c kexec_purgatory < arch/x86/purgatory/purgatory.ro > arch/x86/purgatory/kexec-purgatory.c' > arch/x86/purgatory/.kexec-purgatory.c.cmd
set -e; 	   echo '  CC      arch/x86/purgatory/kexec-purgatory.o'; gcc -Wp,-MD,arch/x86/purgatory/.kexec-purgatory.o.d  -nostdinc -isystem /usr/lib/gcc/x86_64-linux-gnu/8/include -I./arch/x86/include -I./arch/x86/include/generated  -I./include -I./arch/x86/include/uapi -I./arch/x86/include/generated/uapi -I./include/uapi -I./include/generated/uapi -include ./include/linux/kconfig.h -include ./include/linux/compiler_types.h -D__KERNEL__ -fno-strict-aliasing -Wall -Wstrict-prototypes -fno-zero-initialized-in-bss -fno-builtin -ffreestanding -c -Os -mcmodel=large -m64 -fno-PIE    -DKBUILD_BASENAME='"kexec_purgatory"' -DKBUILD_MODNAME='"kexec_purgatory"' -c -o arch/x86/purgatory/.tmp_kexec-purgatory.o arch/x86/purgatory/kexec-purgatory.c; scripts/basic/fixdep arch/x86/purgatory/.kexec-purgatory.o.d arch/x86/purgatory/kexec-purgatory.o 'gcc -Wp,-MD,arch/x86/purgatory/.kexec-purgatory.o.d  -nostdinc -isystem /usr/lib/gcc/x86_64-linux-gnu/8/include -I./arch/x86/include -I./arch/x86/include/generated  -I./include -I./arch/x86/include/uapi -I./arch/x86/include/generated/uapi -I./include/uapi -I./include/generated/uapi -include ./include/linux/kconfig.h -include ./include/linux/compiler_types.h -D__KERNEL__ -fno-strict-aliasing -Wall -Wstrict-prototypes -fno-zero-initialized-in-bss -fno-builtin -ffreestanding -c -Os -mcmodel=large -m64 -fno-PIE    -DKBUILD_BASENAME='\''"kexec_purgatory"'\'' -DKBUILD_MODNAME='\''"kexec_purgatory"'\'' -c -o arch/x86/purgatory/.tmp_kexec-purgatory.o arch/x86/purgatory/kexec-purgatory.c' > arch/x86/purgatory/.kexec-purgatory.o.tmp; rm -f arch/x86/purgatory/.kexec-purgatory.o.d; mv -f arch/x86/purgatory/.kexec-purgatory.o.tmp arch/x86/purgatory/.kexec-purgatory.o.cmd;    if objdump -h arch/x86/purgatory/.tmp_kexec-purgatory.o | grep -q __ksymtab; then gcc -E -D__GENKSYMS__ -Wp,-MD,arch/x86/purgatory/.kexec-purgatory.o.d  -nostdinc -isystem /usr/lib/gcc/x86_64-linux-gnu/8/include -I./arch/x86/include -I./arch/x86/include/generated  -I./include -I./arch/x86/include/uapi -I./arch/x86/include/generated/uapi -I./include/uapi -I./include/generated/uapi -include ./include/linux/kconfig.h -include ./include/linux/compiler_types.h -D__KERNEL__ -fno-strict-aliasing -Wall -Wstrict-prototypes -fno-zero-initialized-in-bss -fno-builtin -ffreestanding -c -Os -mcmodel=large -m64 -fno-PIE    -DKBUILD_BASENAME='"kexec_purgatory"' -DKBUILD_MODNAME='"kexec_purgatory"' arch/x86/purgatory/kexec-purgatory.c | scripts/genksyms/genksyms    -r /dev/null > arch/x86/purgatory/.tmp_kexec-purgatory.ver; ld -m elf_x86_64  -z max-page-size=0x200000 -r -o arch/x86/purgatory/kexec-purgatory.o arch/x86/purgatory/.tmp_kexec-purgatory.o -T arch/x86/purgatory/.tmp_kexec-purgatory.ver; rm -f arch/x86/purgatory/.tmp_kexec-purgatory.o arch/x86/purgatory/.tmp_kexec-purgatory.ver; else mv -f arch/x86/purgatory/.tmp_kexec-purgatory.o arch/x86/purgatory/kexec-purgatory.o; fi;  
set -e;  echo '  AR      arch/x86/purgatory/built-in.a'; rm -f arch/x86/purgatory/built-in.a; ar rcSTPD arch/x86/purgatory/built-in.a arch/x86/purgatory/kexec-purgatory.o; printf '%s\n' 'cmd_arch/x86/purgatory/built-in.a := rm -f arch/x86/purgatory/built-in.a; ar rcSTPD arch/x86/purgatory/built-in.a arch/x86/purgatory/kexec-purgatory.o' > arch/x86/purgatory/.built-in.a.cmd

set -e;  echo '  LDS     arch/x86/realmode/rm/realmode.lds'; gcc -E -Wp,-MD,arch/x86/realmode/rm/.realmode.lds.d  -nostdinc -isystem /usr/lib/gcc/x86_64-linux-gnu/8/include -I./arch/x86/include -I./arch/x86/include/generated  -I./include -I./arch/x86/include/uapi -I./arch/x86/include/generated/uapi -I./include/uapi -I./include/generated/uapi -include ./include/linux/kconfig.h -D__KERNEL__     -P -C -I./arch/x86/realmode/rm -P -Ux86 -D__ASSEMBLY__ -DLINKER_SCRIPT -o arch/x86/realmode/rm/realmode.lds arch/x86/realmode/rm/realmode.lds.S; scripts/basic/fixdep arch/x86/realmode/rm/.realmode.lds.d arch/x86/realmode/rm/realmode.lds 'gcc -E -Wp,-MD,arch/x86/realmode/rm/.realmode.lds.d  -nostdinc -isystem /usr/lib/gcc/x86_64-linux-gnu/8/include -I./arch/x86/include -I./arch/x86/include/generated  -I./include -I./arch/x86/include/uapi -I./arch/x86/include/generated/uapi -I./include/uapi -I./include/generated/uapi -include ./include/linux/kconfig.h -D__KERNEL__     -P -C -I./arch/x86/realmode/rm -P -Ux86 -D__ASSEMBLY__ -DLINKER_SCRIPT -o arch/x86/realmode/rm/realmode.lds arch/x86/realmode/rm/realmode.lds.S' > arch/x86/realmode/rm/.realmode.lds.tmp; rm -f arch/x86/realmode/rm/.realmode.lds.d; mv -f arch/x86/realmode/rm/.realmode.lds.tmp arch/x86/realmode/rm/.realmode.lds.cmd;
set -e;  echo '  LD      arch/x86/realmode/rm/realmode.elf'; ld -m elf_x86_64  -z max-page-size=0x200000   --emit-relocs -T arch/x86/realmode/rm/realmode.lds arch/x86/realmode/rm/header.o arch/x86/realmode/rm/trampoline_64.o arch/x86/realmode/rm/stack.o arch/x86/realmode/rm/reboot.o arch/x86/realmode/rm/wakeup_asm.o arch/x86/realmode/rm/wakemain.o arch/x86/realmode/rm/video-mode.o arch/x86/realmode/rm/copy.o arch/x86/realmode/rm/bioscall.o arch/x86/realmode/rm/regs.o arch/x86/realmode/rm/video-vga.o arch/x86/realmode/rm/video-vesa.o arch/x86/realmode/rm/video-bios.o -o arch/x86/realmode/rm/realmode.elf; printf '%s\n' 'cmd_arch/x86/realmode/rm/realmode.elf := ld -m elf_x86_64  -z max-page-size=0x200000   --emit-relocs -T arch/x86/realmode/rm/realmode.lds arch/x86/realmode/rm/header.o arch/x86/realmode/rm/trampoline_64.o arch/x86/realmode/rm/stack.o arch/x86/realmode/rm/reboot.o arch/x86/realmode/rm/wakeup_asm.o arch/x86/realmode/rm/wakemain.o arch/x86/realmode/rm/video-mode.o arch/x86/realmode/rm/copy.o arch/x86/realmode/rm/bioscall.o arch/x86/realmode/rm/regs.o arch/x86/realmode/rm/video-vga.o arch/x86/realmode/rm/video-vesa.o arch/x86/realmode/rm/video-bios.o -o arch/x86/realmode/rm/realmode.elf' > arch/x86/realmode/rm/.realmode.elf.cmd
set -e;  echo '  RELOCS  arch/x86/realmode/rm/realmode.relocs'; arch/x86/tools/relocs --realmode arch/x86/realmode/rm/realmode.elf > arch/x86/realmode/rm/realmode.relocs; printf '%s\n' 'cmd_arch/x86/realmode/rm/realmode.relocs := arch/x86/tools/relocs --realmode arch/x86/realmode/rm/realmode.elf > arch/x86/realmode/rm/realmode.relocs' > arch/x86/realmode/rm/.realmode.relocs.cmd
set -e;  echo '  OBJCOPY arch/x86/realmode/rm/realmode.bin'; objcopy  -O binary arch/x86/realmode/rm/realmode.elf arch/x86/realmode/rm/realmode.bin; printf '%s\n' 'cmd_arch/x86/realmode/rm/realmode.bin := objcopy  -O binary arch/x86/realmode/rm/realmode.elf arch/x86/realmode/rm/realmode.bin' > arch/x86/realmode/rm/.realmode.bin.cmd

rm -f arch/x86/boot/compressed/.piggy.o.d; mv -f arch/x86/boot/compressed/.piggy.o.tmp arch/x86/boot/compressed/.piggy.o.cmd;   if objdump -h arch/x86/boot/compressed/.tmp_piggy.o | grep -q __ksymtab; then (echo "#include <linux/kernel.h>" ; echo "#include <asm/asm-prototypes.h>" ; gcc -E -Wp,-MD,arch/x86/boot/compressed/.piggy.o.d  -nostdinc -isystem /usr/lib/gcc/x86_64-linux-gnu/8/include -I./arch/x86/include -I./arch/x86/include/generated  -I./include -I./arch/x86/include/uapi -I./arch/x86/include/generated/uapi -I./include/uapi -I./include/generated/uapi -include ./include/linux/kconfig.h -D__KERNEL__ -m64 -O2 -fno-strict-aliasing -fPIE -DDISABLE_BRANCH_PROFILING -mcmodel=small -mno-mmx -mno-sse -ffreestanding -fno-stack-protector -Wno-pointer-sign -D__ASSEMBLY__   arch/x86/boot/compressed/piggy.S | grep "\<___EXPORT_SYMBOL\>" | sed 's/.*___EXPORT_SYMBOL[[:space:]]*\([a-zA-Z0-9_]*\)[[:space:]]*,.*/EXPORT_SYMBOL(\1);/' ) | gcc -E -D__GENKSYMS__ -Wp,-MD,arch/x86/boot/compressed/.piggy.o.d  -nostdinc -isystem /usr/lib/gcc/x86_64-linux-gnu/8/include -I./arch/x86/include -I./arch/x86/include/generated  -I./include -I./arch/x86/include/uapi -I./arch/x86/include/generated/uapi -I./include/uapi -I./include/generated/uapi -include ./include/linux/kconfig.h -include ./include/linux/compiler_types.h -D__KERNEL__ -m64 -O2 -fno-strict-aliasing -fPIE -DDISABLE_BRANCH_PROFILING -mcmodel=small -mno-mmx -mno-sse -ffreestanding -fno-stack-protector -Wno-pointer-sign    -DKBUILD_BASENAME='"piggy"' -DKBUILD_MODNAME='"piggy"' -xc - | scripts/genksyms/genksyms    -r /dev/null > arch/x86/boot/compressed/.tmp_piggy.ver; ld -m elf_x86_64 -z noreloc-overflow -pie --no-dynamic-linker -r -o arch/x86/boot/compressed/piggy.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/.tmp_piggy.o -T arch/x86/boot/compressed/.tmp_piggy.ver; rm -f arch/x86/boot/compressed/.tmp_piggy.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/.tmp_piggy.ver; else mv -f arch/x86/boot/compressed/.tmp_piggy.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/piggy.o; fi;

set -e;  echo '  LD      arch/x86/boot/compressed/vmlinux'; 	for obj in arch/x86/boot/compressed/head_64.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/misc.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/string.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/cmdline.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/error.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/piggy.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/cpuflags.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/early_serial_console.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/kaslr.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/kaslr_64.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/mem_encrypt.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/pgtable_64.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/eboot.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/efi_stub_64.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/efi_thunk_64.o; do readelf -S $obj | grep -qF .rel.local && { echo "error: $obj has data relocations!" >&2; exit 1; } || true; done; ld -m elf_x86_64 -z noreloc-overflow -pie --no-dynamic-linker   -T arch/x86/boot/compressed/vmlinux.lds arch/x86/boot/compressed/head_64.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/misc.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/string.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/cmdline.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/error.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/piggy.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/cpuflags.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/early_serial_console.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/kaslr.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/kaslr_64.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/mem_encrypt.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/pgtable_64.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/eboot.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/efi_stub_64.o drivers/firmware/efi/libstub/lib.a arch/x86/boot/compressed/efi_thunk_64.o -o arch/x86/boot/compressed/vmlinux; printf '%s\n' 'cmd_arch/x86/boot/compressed/vmlinux := 	for obj in arch/x86/boot/compressed/head_64.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/misc.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/string.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/cmdline.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/error.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/piggy.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/cpuflags.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/early_serial_console.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/kaslr.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/kaslr_64.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/mem_encrypt.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/pgtable_64.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/eboot.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/efi_stub_64.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/efi_thunk_64.o; do readelf -S $$obj | grep -qF .rel.local && { echo "error: $$obj has data relocations!" >&2; exit 1; } || true; done; ld -m elf_x86_64 -z noreloc-overflow -pie --no-dynamic-linker   -T arch/x86/boot/compressed/vmlinux.lds arch/x86/boot/compressed/head_64.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/misc.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/string.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/cmdline.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/error.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/piggy.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/cpuflags.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/early_serial_console.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/kaslr.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/kaslr_64.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/mem_encrypt.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/pgtable_64.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/eboot.o arch/x86/boot/compressed/efi_stub_64.o drivers/firmware/efi/libstub/lib.a arch/x86/boot/compressed/efi_thunk_64.o -o arch/x86/boot/compressed/vmlinux' > arch/x86/boot/compressed/.vmlinux.cmd

set -e; 	 echo '  AS      arch/x86/boot/header.o'; gcc -Wp,-MD,arch/x86/boot/.header.o.d  -nostdinc -isystem /usr/lib/gcc/x86_64-linux-gnu/8/include -I./arch/x86/include -I./arch/x86/include/generated  -I./include -I./arch/x86/include/uapi -I./arch/x86/include/generated/uapi -I./include/uapi -I./include/generated/uapi -include ./include/linux/kconfig.h -D__KERNEL__ -m16 -g -Os -DDISABLE_BRANCH_PROFILING -Wall -Wstrict-prototypes -march=i386 -mregparm=3 -fno-strict-aliasing -fomit-frame-pointer -fno-pic -mno-mmx -mno-sse -ffreestanding -fno-stack-protector -mpreferred-stack-boundary=2 -D_SETUP -D__ASSEMBLY__ -DSVGA_MODE=NORMAL_VGA -I./arch/x86/boot   -c -o arch/x86/boot/.tmp_header.o arch/x86/boot/header.S; scripts/basic/fixdep arch/x86/boot/.header.o.d arch/x86/boot/header.o 'gcc -Wp,-MD,arch/x86/boot/.header.o.d  -nostdinc -isystem /usr/lib/gcc/x86_64-linux-gnu/8/include -I./arch/x86/include -I./arch/x86/include/generated  -I./include -I./arch/x86/include/uapi -I./arch/x86/include/generated/uapi -I./include/uapi -I./include/generated/uapi -include ./include/linux/kconfig.h -D__KERNEL__ -m16 -g -Os -DDISABLE_BRANCH_PROFILING -Wall -Wstrict-prototypes -march=i386 -mregparm=3 -fno-strict-aliasing -fomit-frame-pointer -fno-pic -mno-mmx -mno-sse -ffreestanding -fno-stack-protector -mpreferred-stack-boundary=2 -D_SETUP -D__ASSEMBLY__ -DSVGA_MODE=NORMAL_VGA -I./arch/x86/boot   -c -o arch/x86/boot/.tmp_header.o arch/x86/boot/header.S' > arch/x86/boot/.header.o.tmp; echo "#include <asm/asm-prototypes.h>" ; gcc -E -Wp,-MD,arch/x86/boot/.header.o.d  -nostdinc -isystem /usr/lib/gcc/x86_64-linux-gnu/8/include -I./arch/x86/include -I./arch/x86/include/generated  -I./include -I./arch/x86/include/uapi -I./arch/x86/include/generated/uapi -I./include/uapi -I./include/generated/uapi -include ./include/linux/kconfig.h -D__KERNEL__ -m16 -g -Os -DDISABLE_BRANCH_PROFILING -Wall -Wstrict-prototypes -march=i386 -mregparm=3 -fno-strict-aliasing -fomit-frame-pointer -fno-pic -mno-mmx -mno-sse -ffreestanding -fno-stack-protector -mpreferred-stack-boundary=2 -D_SETUP -D__ASSEMBLY__ -DSVGA_MODE=NORMAL_VGA -I./arch/x86/boot   arch/x86/boot/header.S | grep "\<___EXPORT_SYMBOL\>" | sed 's/.*___EXPORT_SYMBOL[[:space:]]*\([a-zA-Z0-9_]*\)[[:space:]]*,.*/EXPORT_SYMBOL(\1);/' ) | gcc -E -D__GENKSYMS__ -Wp,-MD,arch/x86/boot/.header.o.d  -nostdinc -isystem /usr/lib/gcc/x86_64-linux-gnu/8/include -I./arch/x86/include -I./arch/x86/include/generated  -I./include -I./arch/x86/include/uapi -I./arch/x86/include/generated/uapi -I./include/uapi -I./include/generated/uapi -include ./include/linux/kconfig.h -include ./include/linux/compiler_types.h -D__KERNEL__ -m16 -g -Os -DDISABLE_BRANCH_PROFILING -Wall -Wstrict-prototypes -march=i386 -mregparm=3 -fno-strict-aliasing -fomit-frame-pointer -fno-pic -mno-mmx -mno-sse -ffreestanding -fno-stack-protector -mpreferred-stack-boundary=2 -D_SETUP    -DKBUILD_BASENAME='"header"' -DKBUILD_MODNAME='"header"' -xc - | scripts/genksyms/genksyms    -r /dev/null > arch/x86/boot/.tmp_header.ver; ld -m elf_x86_64  -z max-page-size=0x200000 -r -o arch/x86/boot/header.o arch/x86/boot/.tmp_header.o -T arch/x86/boot/.tmp_header.ver; rm -f arch/x86/boot/.tmp_header.o arch/x86/boot/.tmp_header.ver; set -e;  echo '  LD      arch/x86/boot/setup.elf'; ld -m elf_x86_64  -z max-page-size=0x200000   -T arch/x86/boot/setup.ld arch/x86/boot/a20.o arch/x86/boot/bioscall.o arch/x86/boot/cmdline.o arch/x86/boot/copy.o arch/x86/boot/cpu.o arch/x86/boot/cpuflags.o arch/x86/boot/cpucheck.o arch/x86/boot/early_serial_console.o arch/x86/boot/edd.o arch/x86/boot/header.o arch/x86/boot/main.o arch/x86/boot/memory.o arch/x86/boot/pm.o arch/x86/boot/pmjump.o arch/x86/boot/printf.o arch/x86/boot/regs.o arch/x86/boot/string.o arch/x86/boot/tty.o arch/x86/boot/video.o arch/x86/boot/video-mode.o arch/x86/boot/version.o arch/x86/boot/video-vga.o arch/x86/boot/video-vesa.o arch/x86/boot/video-bios.o -o arch/x86/boot/setup.elf; printf '%s\n' 'cmd_arch/x86/boot/setup.elf := ld -m elf_x86_64  -z max-page-size=0x200000   -T arch/x86/boot/setup.ld arch/x86/boot/a20.o arch/x86/boot/bioscall.o arch/x86/boot/cmdline.o arch/x86/boot/copy.o arch/x86/boot/cpu.o arch/x86/boot/cpuflags.o arch/x86/boot/cpucheck.o arch/x86/boot/early_serial_console.o arch/x86/boot/edd.o arch/x86/boot/header.o arch/x86/boot/main.o arch/x86/boot/memory.o arch/x86/boot/pm.o arch/x86/boot/pmjump.o arch/x86/boot/printf.o arch/x86/boot/regs.o arch/x86/boot/string.o arch/x86/boot/tty.o arch/x86/boot/video.o arch/x86/boot/video-mode.o arch/x86/boot/version.o arch/x86/boot/video-vga.o arch/x86/boot/video-vesa.o arch/x86/boot/video-bios.o -o arch/x86/boot/setup.elf' > arch/x86/boot/.setup.elf.cmd
set -e;  echo '  OBJCOPY arch/x86/boot/setup.bin'; objcopy  -O binary arch/x86/boot/setup.elf arch/x86/boot/setup.bin; printf '%s\n' 'cmd_arch/x86/boot/setup.bin := objcopy  -O binary arch/x86/boot/setup.elf arch/x86/boot/setup.bin' > arch/x86/boot/.setup.bin.cmd

set -e;  echo '  BUILD   arch/x86/boot/bzImage'; arch/x86/boot/tools/build arch/x86/boot/setup.bin arch/x86/boot/vmlinux.bin arch/x86/boot/zoffset.h arch/x86/boot/bzImage ; printf '%s\n' 'cmd_arch/x86/boot/bzImage := arch/x86/boot/tools/build arch/x86/boot/setup.bin arch/x86/boot/vmlinux.bin arch/x86/boot/zoffset.h arch/x86/boot/bzImage ' > arch/x86/boot/.bzImage.cmd
echo 'Kernel: arch/x86/boot/bzImage is ready' ' (#'`cat .version`')'
mkdir -p ./arch/x86_64/boot
ln -fsn ../../x86/boot/bzImage ./arch/x86_64/boot/bzImage
